[30;1m409 | [0m[35mFinally, for each format that is already supported by other plugins, add the new plugin[0m
[30;1m410 | [0m[35mat the end of the ``priority`` list. (This avoids breaking existing downstream code.)[0m
[30;1m411 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m412 | [0m[35m[0m
